Cisco ^OxIZ8MPP

Synchronous communication is characterised by "real time" communications. Although the
messages are considered to be real time, they are never really fully real time per se,
there is always a small delay given by the tool, for example the time to press enter
on a chat and the technology, so the time for the message to travel from one place
to the other.
What matters is that the users are online at the same time and do not perceive the
presence of this delay when they communicate.
There are different tools for real time communications and sometimes they are similar
so de distinction can be fuzzy ^w9byeoCt

Text chat is an asynchronous communication tool, messages
appears on the screen of the receiver either when the other press
enter or as they are typed (more real time than the other). Seeing the
message being typed can make the communication feel more alive but at
the same time can cause confusion of many people writing at the same
time or replying to a question while someone is already asking another one.
There are definitely risks associated with text chats, for example
impersonating, grooming and bullying are the most dangerous, especially
for younger people but they are also kinda shared between all online
communications in a way ^7JX2xrQ1

Instant messaging is similar to text chat but it has some additional features. First of
all you usually have a contact list and you can see who is online and who isn't (sometimes 
you can also change your own status to let others know), also the user in this systems
act as the client and contact a server called IM server. The clients are always running
and this let us see the current status of other users. Some examples are Facebook
messenger and skype. While this is great it also create a much more distracting system
 ^EeFSe2Hi

The probably most famous in recent times form of synchronous communication is
video and web conferences. They require to stream video and audio between the
users, the best examples are Zoom, Teams and Skype. This type of communication
require a lot of bandwidth, especially for video, even thought different scientific
studies shows that the benefits of video over audio are unclear. Maintaining
this type of performance is very difficult, you have to weight the quality with
the bandwidth that will be required, in particular we say the gap should not be above
150ms. The process require to establish a connection between the 2 endpoints which
are the combinations of Hw and software. They will need to agree on a frame rate
and a data rate (both chan change during communication), usually frame rate is
15 or 30 while data rate is always more than 500kbps. Once this is done, the
endpoints are ready to send frames to each other, each frame is always
pre-processed before being sent, first with some lossy compression and than with
some algorithms for prediction of the changes in the next frame ^mlDhA0wi

Telepresence is basically video conference on steroids.
It is invented by CISCO and it is a full system, a whole
room to be precise, made to feel as much as possible as 
if the other person is actually in the room with you. This
require taking into account light, sound, image distance
image size and much more. For this reason it is very expensive
and made only for businesses ^KBg5c60u
